jyellick
2016-05-03 12:49
@sheehan Looks like it was a timeout problem, see my passing PR above

simon
2016-05-03 15:12
what's the difference between errored and failed?

ramesh
2016-05-03 15:21
Errored -- If any build exit with non -zero before "script" section, travis consider it as errored and exit from that step

ramesh
2016-05-03 15:22
If any unit tests fails, Travis will not go further and exit

ramesh
2016-05-03 15:23
Fail - This applicable for Script section in travis yml file.. If one of the test case fails, it will continue further and final build status will show as "FAILED"

2016-05-04 14:43
oh yeah.
